--- SUGGESTED PAPER TEXT ---

"We trained a logistic regression model using 80% of text pairs 
(4,765,140 observations) and evaluated on a held-out 
test set of 1,191,286 pairs (20%). Ten-fold cross-validation 
on the training set yielded ROC AUC = 0.78 
(SD = 0.00). On the held-out test set, 
the model achieved ROC AUC = 0.78, confirming 
generalization to unseen data.

Using Shapley value decomposition to assess relative feature contributions 
(accounting for collinearity), hapax legomena contribute 85%, 
SVM stylometry 13%, and sequence alignment 
2%. All predictors are statistically 
significant (p < 0.001)."
